### Key Findings

**The Pattern**: In Kafka, `ConfigDef` and `ConfigDef.ConfigKey` (a static inner class) form the configuration documentation pattern. `ConfigKey` annotates each config key with its type, default value, importance, documentation string, and validation rules. `ConfigDef` provides documentation generation methods (`toHtml()`, `toEnrichedRst()`, `toHtmlTable()`).

**Core Definitions** (the "annotation definitions"):
- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/ConfigDef.java` — defines `ConfigDef` class and `ConfigKey` inner class
